*Quale e una parte della collana mostrata*

![[src_kangourou_2019_koala_preecolier__prob2.png]]

> Gli allievi segnano le loro risposte sul fascicolo dei quesiti (si suggerisce di far compilare sulla prima
> facciata la classe e nome e cognome); poi lo consegnano al docente, che provvede a compilare tutte
> le schede da inviare per la valutazione.
> In ogni caso spetta al docente compilare la parte relativa al tempo impiegato dall’allievo.
> Ogni scheda-risposta che invierete per la valutazione dovrà essere letta da un lettore ottico: per questo si devono usare solo penne di colore NERO. Per individuare una casella, non basta tracciarvi una
> croce sopra: occorre che venga annerita per intero e senza sbavature, come mostra il fac-simile nella
> pagina a fianco, relativo ad un’ipotetica allieva che
> -
> si chiama BACE ADA (nella prima colonna del “campo 1”  va quindi annerita la casella a destra
> della lettera “B”, nella seconda colonna quella a destra della lettera “A” e così via; va lasciata in bianco la colonna relativa allo spazio tra cognome e nome, che vanno inseriti in questo ordine);
> -
> ha risposto solo ai quesiti n. 1, 2, 3, 4, 6, 9 dando rispettivamente le risposte A, B, B, C, A, E;
> -
> frequenta la classe II della scuola elementare “ALESSANDRO VOLTA”;
> -
> ha consegnato al docente le sue risposte dopo 42 minuti.
> Non sono ammesse correzioni e/o cancellature (le schede sono comunque fornite in sovrannumero).
> PUNTEGGI
> Come si attribuisce il punteggio:
> Quindi, se un quesito vale di più, sbagliarne la risposta costa di più.  Ad esempio, se si risponde a tutti
> i quesiti e in modo corretto a tutti tranne 
> •
> uno da 3 punti, si ottengono 3x7 + 4x8 + 5x8 - 0,75 = 92,25 punti
> •
> uno da 4 punti, si ottengono 3x8 + 4x7 + 5x8 - 1      = 91 punti 
> •
> uno da 5 punti, si ottengono 3x8 + 4x8 + 5x7 - 1,25 = 89,75 punti.
> Si ribadisce che per ogni quesito una e una sola delle cinque risposte indicate è corretta. 
> Quesiti
> Risposta Esatta
> Risposta Errata
> Nessuna risposta
> dal N. 1 al N. 8
> + 3 punti
> - 0,75 punti
> 0 punti
> dal N. 9 al N. 16
> + 4 punti
> - 1 punto
> 0 punti
> dal N. 17 al N. 24
> + 5 punti
> - 1,25 punti
> 0 punti
> -
> o
> a
> e
> -
> a
> a
> a
> -
> .
> i
> 
> 22
> Le malizie dei Koala n° 6

> KOALA 2019
> 
> 21
> Le malizie dei Koala n° 6
> GIOCO KOALA •
> I testi possono essere letti da un adulto.
> Per ogni quesito, tra le 5 risposte proposte, una
> sola è giusta. Metti una croce nel koala posto a
> fianco o sotto la risposta che ritieni giusta.
> 1
> B 
> C 
> D
> E 
> A
> Quale di questi cinque rettangoli 
> contiene soltanto numeri minori di 7?
> 6
> 1
> 7
> 8
> 6
> 2
> 7
> 4
> 5
> 2
> 9
> 3
> 1
> 3
> 5
> 2
> 10
> 8
> 7
> 9
> 2
> Osserva questa collana.    
> Quale di queste è una sua parte?   
> A
> B
> C
> D
> E
> 4
> B 
> C 
> D
> E 
> A
> 8
> 6
> 5
> 4
> 3
> In figura vedi delle calze, su ognuna 
> delle quali è riportato un numero. 
> Per comporre un paio, si devono usare

< MSK0/>Which and part of the necklace shown< MSK1/>

![[src_kangourou_2019_koala_preecolier__prob2.png]]

> The students mark their answers on the questionnaire (it is suggested that the class and name and surname be completed on the first face); they then hand it over to the teacher, who will fill out all the sheets to be sent for the assessment. In any case, the teacher is responsible for completing the part relating to the time spent by the pupil. Each reply sheet you submit for evaluation must be read by an optical reader, so only NERO pencils are required. To locate a box, it is not enough to draw a cross over it: it must be blackened entirely and without scratches, as shown by the facsimile on the next page, relating to a hypothetical pupil who - is called BACE ADA (in the first column of the field 1 the box to the right of the letter B, in the second column the one to the right of the letter A and so on; the column relating to the space between surname and name, which must be entered in this order only) - has answered questions n. 1, 2, 3, 4, 6, 9 giving the answers A, B, B, C, A, E respectively; - attends class II of the primary school ALESSANDRO VOLTA; - delivered his answers to the teacher after 42 minutes. No corrections and/or cancellations are allowed (the tables are however sub-numbered). How to score: So if a question is worth more, the wrong answer costs more. For example, if you answer all the questions and correctly answer all but • one from 3 points, you get 3x7 + 4x8 + 5x8 - 0.75 = 92.25 points • one from 4 points, you get 3x8 + 4x7 + 5x8 - 1 = 91 points • one from 5 points, you get 3x8 + 4x8 + 5x7 - 1.25 = 89.75 points. It is reiterated that for each question only one of the five answers given is correct. Questions Answered correct Answered wrong No answer from N. 1 al N. 8 + 3 points - 0,75 points 0 points from N. 9 al N. 16 + 4 points - 1 point 0 points from N. 17 al N. 24 + 5 points - 1.25 points 0 points - or a e - a a - . i

> V O L T A B A C E A D A <K> KOALA 2019
> 
> • The text can be read by an adult. For each question, out of the five proposed answers, only one is correct. Put a cross in the koala next to or underneath the answer you think is right. 1 B C D E A Which of these five rectangles contains only numbers less than 7? 6 1 7 8 6 2 7 4 5 2 9 3 1 3 5 2 10 8 7 9 2 Look at this necklace. Which one of these is his share? A B C D E 4 B C D E A 8 6 5 4 3 In the figure you can see socks, each of which has a number. To make a pair, you have to use two socks with the same number. How many pairs of socks can you make? 8 5 7 3 5 7 1 6 1 2 3 2 3 Catherine cut a piece of this grid.
>  
> B C D E A Which one of these could be the piece he cut?
>  
> 
> 20 The Koala's Malizes n° 6 GIOCO KOALA • 5 B C D E A 8 7 6 5 4 By gluing a triangle and discs all equal to each other on a cardboard, possibly broken in half, Marco created the image of a small house. To make fun of him, Anna took away some of the entire disks. The figure shows you what remains of Mark's work. How many floppy disks did Anna take? To form a flower cluster, Gaia must use all the flowers that are in the rectangle, but outside the triangle, and only those. How many flowers will Gaia's deck be made of? 26 22 19 14 13 8 C E B D A On the conveyor belt to the left of the figure, the packages are aligned. When the three tapes begin to move, the elf alternately distributes the packets on the right D tape and on the left S tape: the first pack goes on the right one, the second on the left one, the third on the right tape, the fourth on the left one, and so on. When the distribution is over, all tapes will stop. Which of these figures shows you how the packages will be aligned on the left-hand tape? D S 7 B E C D A ... We're going to cost six cents together. We're together for eight cents. How many cents? You and I together? 5 6 7 8 9 Questions from N. 1 al N. 8 is worth 3 points.
> 
> 19 Koala Diseases n< MSK0/> 6 KOALA GAME • The text can be read by an adult. For each question, out of the five proposed answers, only one is correct. Put a cross in the koala next to or underneath the answer you think is right. 9 If you want to keep the mouse from reaching the cheese, you just need to close two doors. What kind? C D E A B 1 and 2 3 and 4 3 and 5 4 and 5 2 and 3 10 B C D E A Patricia had a sheet of paper. He folded it once and then a second along the stretched segments and finally cut it along the unstretched segment: these three operations are suggested to you in the order from the figure. How many pieces of paper did you get?
>       
> 2 3 4 5 6 12 B C D E A The figure shows you a square floor of 9 tiles, a cat and a cup of milk occupying tiles placed at two opposite corners of the square. The cat can only move in the directions indicated by the arrows, that is, from left to right or from top to bottom, and if it wants to change direction, it can only do so when it is in the center of a tile. How many different routes do they take to get to the cup of milk? 2 3 4 5 6 11 B C D E A Five square sheets of paper, of different colour and numbered, are partially overlapped to form a single square, as shown in the figure. Sandra wants to pick them up one at a time, but to pick up a sheet, no one else needs to cover even a part of it. In what order do you have to take them?
>  
> 4-5-2-3-1 1-2-3-4-5 5-2-3-4-1 5-2-3-1-4 5-3-2-1-4
> 
> 18 Koala straps n< MSK0/> 6 KOALA GAME • 13 Four strips of paper are interwoven and glued to a transparent glass; Silvia and Aldo observe them from opposite sides of the glass. The figure shows you what Silvia sees. What does Aldo see? B C D E A 14 B C D E A Corrado wants to paste four equal cubes together and then paint the solid that he composed, but the little paint that he has is enough for only one of the five solids that he could make up. What kind?
>    
> 16 B C D E A A train left Kang at 6 o'clock in the morning, heading for Aroo (a place very far from Kang) where it arrived at 11 o'clock in the evening. During the journey he made three intermediate stops: the numbers shown in the figure indicate, in order, the travel times between Kang and the first stop, those between the first stop and the second, those between the second and the third. How many hours did it take you to get from the third stop to Aroo? KANG AROO two three seven ? 6 2 3 4 5 15 The figure shows you a rectangular floor obtained by attaching some rectangular plates, all of them equal to each other. The shortest side of each plate is one meter long. How long is the longest side of the floor? B C D E A6 8 10 11 12 1m ? The questions from N. 9 al N. 16 is worth 4 points.
> 
> 17 Koala Diseases n< MSK0/> 6 KOALA GAMES • The text can be read by an adult. For each question, out of the five proposed answers, only one is correct. Put a cross in the koala next to or underneath the answer you think is right. 17 On a farm there are only sheep and cows. The fattening factor combines one cow and one sheep at a time: thus, when all the cows are fattening, eight sheep remain to be fattened. The total number of sheep is twice that of cows. How many animals are there on the farm?
>  
> B C D E A16 18 20 24 28 18 B C D E A Cutting a figure, Mauro got the three pieces you see. Which of the following is the figure that Mauro cut? 20 B C D E A2 3 4 5 6 Three squirrels together found 7 nuts. Each found a different number of nuts than the others, and they all found at least one. How many walnuts did the squirrel find? 19 In the zoo there are some camels with two goblets and some dromedaries with one goblet, 10 animals in all. There are 14 goblins in all. How many dromedaries are there? B C D E A2 3 4 6 7
> 
> 16 Koala Malizes n° 6 KOALA GAME • 21 B C D E A While playing on the beach, Tim and Tom formed a pile of sand and planted a flag on top of it. Exactly half the flag's mast is stuck in the sand; from the top of the mast to the base of the pile of sand there are 80 centimeters, from the base of the mast to the base of the pile there are 20 centimeters. How high is the pile of sand? 40 45 50 55 60 22 Henry came and replaced every black square with a white square. Then Fabio arrived and, in the strip left by Henry, replaced each gray square with a black square. Finally Gino arrived and, in the strip left by Fabio, replaced each white square with a grey square. What's the strip left by Gino? B C D E A Here you see a strip divided into nine squares. 24 B C D E A A strange switch-key machine gives you three white tokens if you put one in red, it gives you two red tokens if you put one in white. At the beginning of the game you have three red and one white tokens. After you've played three times, placing one token at a time, what is the minimum number of chips, between white and red, that you can find yourself having? 7 6 8 5 9 23 B C D E A
>  
> Peter carved out a square of four cells, summed up the four numbers that appear in these four cells, and told you that he got a number greater than 63. Then he told you that at least one of the following five numbers appears in the square that he carved and asked you to guess. Which of these five numbers do you have to indicate if you want to make sure you're not wrong? 10 14 15 8 18 From the numbered grid you see below the questions from N. 17 al N. Twenty-four is worth five points.
